            <h1>Jenna Bush Hager says father George W. Bush is a 'feminist' - as she praises him for inspiring her to raise 'strong' daughters, by always showing her she could be whatever she wanted to be</h1>      
      <ul class="mol-bullets-with-font"><li class=""><strong>The 35-year-old mother-of-two explained in a recent interview that her father and mother raised her and her sister Barbara to be strong and independentÂ </strong></li><li class=""><strong>Jenna added that she believes her father is a feminist - although admitted that some people might 'laugh' at the suggestionÂ </strong></li><li class=""><strong>The Today show host is mother to two daughters - Mila, four, and Poppy, 20 monthsÂ - with her husband Henry Hager</strong></li></ul><p class="author-section byline-plain">By

</p><div itemprop="articleBody"><p class="mol-para-with-font">Jenna Bush Hager has proudly hailed her father, former President George W. <script async src="//cdn.taboola.com/libtrc/dailymail-us/loader.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = 10;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '<div id="' + id + '" style="min-height: 280px;"></div>';
            $(node).before(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n});
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=femail&pageSize=10',
            total: 19.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
</script>
